<span id="freeTextContainer16681468415625773952"><b> 4 Stars</b><br/><br/><b>Overall Opinion: </b>This was a super cute and enjoyable read! I enjoyed it, especially because of the H. I floved him! My heart broke for all that he went through and how misunderstood he was for his time. I also really appreciated how the h cared for him how he was, and never tried to change who he was. I would recommend this for anybody trying out the HR genre. I don't normally read the HR genre, but this has to be one of my favorites so far 😊<br/><br/><b>Brief Summary of the Storyline: </b> This is Beth </span>
  <span id="freeText16681468415625773952" style="display:none"><b> 4 Stars</b><br /><br /><b>Overall Opinion: </b>This was a super cute and enjoyable read! I enjoyed it, especially because of the H. I floved him! My heart broke for all that he went through and how misunderstood he was for his time. I also really appreciated how the h cared for him how he was, and never tried to change who he was. I would recommend this for anybody trying out the HR genre. I don't normally read the HR genre, but this has to be one of my favorites so far 😊<br /><br /><b>Brief Summary of the Storyline: </b> This is Beth and Ian's story. Ian is a collector of Ming bowls, and he meets with an acquaintance that is trying to procure the same one as him. He soon finds out that this acquaintance is planning to marry a newly wealthy widow, Beth. He steps in and warns Beth, because this acquaintance is not what he seems and he starts his strong pursuit of her in his place. There is a police detective that has a bone to pick with Ian's family and starts harassing both him and Beth over a couple of murders. There is a little suspense and mystery, a few laugh-out-loud moments, and some sexy times...and the get a HEA ending.<br /><br /><b>POV:</b> This alternated between focusing mainly on Beth and Ian in 3rd person narrative.<br /><br /><b>Overall Pace of Story: </b> Good. I never skimmed, and I thought it flowed well.<br /><br /><b>Instalove:</b> Kind of. I tolerated it though, because they don't voice their feelings or even realize them themselves until much later.<br /><br /><b>H rating:</b> 5 stars! Ian. I LOVED him! I have a son that has Asperger's Syndrome (high functioning autism), and I am certain Ian was an aspie too ~ which I always love!! <br /><br /><b>h rating:</b> 4 stars. Beth. I liked her spirit and the way she cared about Ian.<br /><br /><b>Sadness level: </b>Low, no tissues needed<br /><br /><b>Push/Pull:</b> Not really <br /><br /><b>Heat level:</b> Good. They have some good tension, chemistry, and scenes -- but not so much it takes away from the story.<br /><br /><b>Descriptive sex:</b> Yes/HR style 😉<br /><br /><b>OW/OM drama:</b> Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[The h is with OM when she meets the H.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Sex scene with OW or OM:</b> No<br /><br /><b>Cheating: </b> No<br /><br /><b>Separation:</b> No<br /><br /><b>Possible Triggers: </b>Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[prostitution/murder (off page - through mentions), loss of a spouse (off page - through memories), and institutionalization/medical experimentation (off page - through memories) <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Closure: </b> This had pretty good closure and a jump ahead epilogue with a HEA ending <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[They get remarried and she is pregnant <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>How I got it:</b> I got it on loan through my public library.<br /><br /><b>Safety:</b> This one should be <u>Safe</u> for most safety gang readers<br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br />- <b>Does Not</b> have cheating<br />- <b>Does Not</b> have a descriptive sex scene with OW/OM<br />- <b> Does Not</b> have the h or H pushing away<br />- <b> Does Not</b> have a separation between the h and H<br />- <b> Does Not</b> have abuse<br />- <b> Does Not</b> have OTT sad parts<br />- <b>Does </b> have a HEA ending <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/510929577?book_show_action=true">Jan 19, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="It&#39;s just me Shelly B" class="user" itemprop="url" name="It&#39;s just me Shelly B" href="/user/show/3716081-it-s-just-me-shelly-b">It&#39;s just me Shelly B</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to It's just me Shelly B by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/8310179-blacky-romance-addict">Blacky *Romance Addict*</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3716081-it-s-just-me-shelly-b?shelf=historical">historical</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer510929577" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16673159152656034730"><b>“You are a rogue and a scoundrel, and I love every single second of it.”</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380405834i/791138._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Lord Ian Mackenzie was deemed a lunatic at an early age by the courts and thrown into an asylum until his brother, the Duke, rescued him a few years later. He is known as the "Mad Mackenzie." He has rages and quirks that most people just can't comprehend in this time in history. He is also extremely intelligent and can remember conversations verbatim. Oh yea did I mention is he tall, gorgeous, protective and sexy as hell? We</span>
  <span id="freeText16673159152656034730" style="display:none"><b>“You are a rogue and a scoundrel, and I love every single second of it.”</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380405834i/791138._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Lord Ian Mackenzie was deemed a lunatic at an early age by the courts and thrown into an asylum until his brother, the Duke, rescued him a few years later. He is known as the "Mad Mackenzie." He has rages and quirks that most people just can't comprehend in this time in history. He is also extremely intelligent and can remember conversations verbatim. Oh yea did I mention is he tall, gorgeous, protective and sexy as hell? Well he is, so go ahead and check those of the list too.<br><br><b>“There, my dear, goes an eccentric.”....“Mad as a hatter. Poor chap lived in a private asylum most of his life, “and he runs free now only because his brother the duke let him out again..."</b><br><br>He does not understand feelings, he can't tell whether people are joking, happy, sad and he doesn't know how to love. <br><br><b>“Explain to me what loving feels like, Beth. I want to understand.”<br><br>“The love for another’s body. But also love for their heart and their mind, and for all the silly things they do, no matter how absurd. Your world brightens when they walk into a room, dims when they leave it again. You want to be with the beloved so you can see him and touch him and hear his voice, but you want his happiness as well. It’s selfish, but not entirely so.”</b><br><br>He meets Beth at the opera and he's immediately drawn to her in the same way that he's drawn to his Ming pottery. He knows she's worth keeping and he will do anything to have her as his wife. <br><br><b>“Your being with me makes it stop. It’s like the Ming bowls—when I touch them and feel them, everything stops. Nothing matters. You are the same.”</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380405834i/791139.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Beth Ackerley is a widow of a vicar and she inherited enough money to be comfortable from an heiress she worked for. She's not really looking for love, just a partner to spend time with. That is until she meets Ian and everything changes for her and I do mean everything. He is just so easy to love...well I think he is anyway. She is also strong, proud and doesn't back down to no one.<br><br><b>“Do I love you?"<br><br>“I never understood before. It’s like fear and hope, both warm and cold. All mixed together.”</b><br><br>So the story begins and it's is so beautiful watching the transformation in Ian. Just little things that we do everyday and take for granted he can't do.....things as simple as eye contact. So watching him learn and want to do things for Beth.....<b>its swoon worthy!!</b><br><br>This book has it all........love, madness, sorrow, suspense, borderline crazy family, family ties, twists, sex, courtesans, and so much more. I LOVED LOVED LOVED this book and I can't wait to start the next one:))<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380405834i/791140.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>“All of us are mad in some way,”</b><br><br>Very well said Ian, we are ALL crazy in our own way!!!!!!!!!! Each and every one of us have issues and quirks that will drive someone crazy. It was very interesting to me and very real how she portrayed the views of mental illness from a stand point in 1881, even a case as Ian's which by today's standard would be considered a mild from of autism...I would think. I can imagine to this very proper society it was deemed crazy and eccentric, where as we probably wouldn't blink an eye to it.<br><br>If you like historical books or are willing to try one, this is the ONE to try....it's absolutely fantastic! I just can't put into words how beautiful it is but read it and find out for yourself!!!!!! I'm going to put in 1 more quote that was my favorite even though it really has no meaning as to the story line other than maybe how Ian's mind works.<br><br><b>“He stared at the droplet, something inside him singing at the perfection of the ball of ink, the glistening viscosity that held it suspended from the nib. The sphere was perfect, shining, a wonder.<br>He wished he could savour its perfection forever, but he knew that in a second it would fall from the pen and be lost."<br><br><i>Buddy read with Vishous......it was verra good V:))))))</i></b></span>

<div id="review_140442309" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/140442309" />
    <a title="Lisa Kay" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2459470-lisa-kay"><img alt="Lisa Kay" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1534570690p2/2459470.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/140442309?book_show_action=true">Jan 13, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lisa Kay" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lisa Kay" href="/user/show/2459470-lisa-kay">Lisa Kay</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2459470-lisa-kay?shelf=genre-romance-historical">genre-romance-historical</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2459470-lisa-kay?shelf=theme-hero-heals-heroine">theme-hero-heals-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2459470-lisa-kay?shelf=authors-j">authors-j</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2459470-lisa-kay?shelf=all-time-favorites">all-time-favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2459470-lisa-kay?shelf=amazing-secondary-characters">amazing-secondary-characters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2459470-lisa-kay?shelf=reviewed-by-me">reviewed-by-me</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2459470-lisa-kay?shelf=authors-a">authors-a</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2459470-lisa-kay?shelf=genre-mystery-subplot">genre-mystery-subplot</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2459470-lisa-kay?shelf=character-widow">character-widow</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2459470-lisa-kay?shelf=series-h">series-h</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer140442309" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9913156974144356303">Wow! How can I rate a book more than five stars? Even after all the hype, this book still held up. I guess all I can do is put it on my “all-time-favorites” bookshelf.<br/><a href='http://s1205.photobucket.com/albums/bb438/LKC55/?action=view&current=7d23b912.jpg' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380343998i/699109.jpg' alt='Lord Ian' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/>Lord Ian is intense and he leaped off the pages and into my arms. I wondered how <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/28569.Jennifer_Ashley' title='Jennifer Ashley' rel='nofollow noopener'>Jennifer Ashley</a> was going to present his POV, since he has Asperger syndrome, and at times it was almost as if it was written by someone else, the tone is so substantially different.<br/><br/>Here is a scene, from the heroine’s POV, from early in the book wh</span>
  <span id="freeText9913156974144356303" style="display:none">Wow! How can I rate a book more than five stars? Even after all the hype, this book still held up. I guess all I can do is put it on my “all-time-favorites” bookshelf.<br><a href="http://s1205.photobucket.com/albums/bb438/LKC55/?action=view&amp;current=7d23b912.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380343998i/699109.jpg" alt="Lord Ian" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>Lord Ian is intense and he leaped off the pages and into my arms. I wondered how <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/28569.Jennifer_Ashley" title="Jennifer Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">Jennifer Ashley</a> was going to present his POV, since he has Asperger syndrome, and at times it was almost as if it was written by someone else, the tone is so substantially different.<br><br>Here is a scene, from the heroine’s POV, from early in the book when the hero, Ian, has just met the heroine, Beth, at the opera for the first time. You can see she is attracted to him, yet he is disconcerting her; while Ian doesn’t know how to take her teasing:<br><blockquote>Lord Ian drew a thin curl between his fingers, straightening it. He let it go, his eyes flickering as it bounced against her forehead. He drew the curl out again, watching it bounce back, and again. His concentration unnerved her; the closeness of his body unnerved her more. At the same time, her own wanton body was responding.<br><br>“You shall take all the spring out of it,” she said. “My maid will be so disappointed.”<br><br>Ian blinked, then returned his hand to the arm of his chair as though having to force it.</blockquote>I liked the humor in the heroine, Beth; it is delicious when she finally makes Ian laugh out loud, something he never does. Still, she is also a tenacious woman out to solve a mystery. It is nice to see a heroine worthy of the hero.<br><br>The three brothers, Isabella, and the servants were very, very real; their dialogues believable. I found the relationship between Ian and Hart thought-provoking. Each brother thinks the other is guilty of something. I loved that Hart, the Duke, was earthy - but also so arrogantly rude to Beth - believing her to be not good enough for his brother, only worried about her safety with regards to how it would affect Ian; conversely, at the same time rude and dismissive toward Ian feelings, while still relying on him for his abilities. On second thought, Hart is rude to <i>everyone</i>. Ms. Ashley has created complex characterizations here and they are fun, intense, emotional and subsequently button-pushing. A wonderful love story about a woman learning to love again and a man, who thinks he can’t, learning to love for the first time!<br><br>Ms. Ashley is a new-to-me-author and I will definitely be purchasing, not borrowing, more of her works.<br></span>
  <a data-text-id="9913156974144356303" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_650654014" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/650654014" />
    <a title="Addie H" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/16858463-addie-h"><img alt="Addie H" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1511793475p2/16858463.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/650654014?book_show_action=true">Jun 25, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Addie H" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Addie H" href="/user/show/16858463-addie-h">Addie H</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16858463-addie-h?shelf=zz-rereadfavs">zz-rereadfavs</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16858463-addie-h?shelf=h-rom-regency">h-rom-regency</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16858463-addie-h?shelf=zo-scar-mental">zo-scar-mental</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer650654014" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16857867659673537728"><b>NB : On kindle sale today 19th May 2020 for USD 2.99</b><br/><br/>I am re-reading all my 5 star rated romance novels. There are 60 on my shelf. This is book 5. <br/><br/><i>(Tropes: Widow, Tortured Hero (Asberger))</i> <br/><br/>This is how my 5th re-read held up. <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1524296943ra/25410724.gif' width='350' height='250' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I LOVE Ian. And I really want Ian to find love, peace and happiness. And for sure he finds that in Beth. So his needs are met. Happy ending for him. YAY!<br/><br/>Beth. Will a man who is emotionally (almost) unavailable, has no filter, can’t lie, can’t look you in the eye, can’t unders</span>
  <span id="freeText16857867659673537728" style="display:none"><b>NB : On kindle sale today 19th May 2020 for USD 2.99</b><br><br>I am re-reading all my 5 star rated romance novels. There are 60 on my shelf. This is book 5. <br><br><i>(Tropes: Widow, Tortured Hero (Asberger))</i> <br><br>This is how my 5th re-read held up. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1524296943ra/25410724.gif" width="350" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I LOVE Ian. And I really want Ian to find love, peace and happiness. And for sure he finds that in Beth. So his needs are met. Happy ending for him. YAY!<br><br>Beth. Will a man who is emotionally (almost) unavailable, has no filter, can’t lie, can’t look you in the eye, can’t understand or is not interested in what you say, be enough in the long run? <br><br>In this book yes…? In the real world? I struggle mightily to see it. <br><br>I want it to be enough, but I certainly could not handle it. I believe that communication and emotional support are some very important keys to a happy relationship. And humor! Beth likes to joke, Ian doesn’t get them. I could never be in a relationship with a guy who does not look at life and burst out laughing. <br><br>While Ian certainly “improves” with Beth’s presence in his life, I don’t see a lot of the benefit in this relationship for her (well, apart from the sex of course…we all know great sex cures all 😊)<br><br>Also, Ian and his brothers are very heavy handed. Beth is constantly dragged, pulled, lifted, pushed, held tight, and ordered about in a way that I have clearly overlooked in the past, but on this reading I found problematic. <br><br>Frankly, I found Ian’s brothers very off-putting. <br><br>This book also threads on my crude tolerance boundary (Ian has no filter). Now I will admit, my crude tolerance is weak, so others might scoff at it, but for me it occasionally pushes the book from romantic and hot into not my kind of porn :D Just not my flavor. (I am talking about the language, not the actual acts.)<br><br>Still, I am really torn, I love so much about this book, and I really don’t like certain things in this book. <br><br>So the re-read dropped from a 5 to a weak 4.<br><br>Doesn’t stop me from quoting some of my favorite moments though.<br><br>************<br><i>- Ian never knew what went on behind people’s expressions. Everyone else instinctively knew the signs of rage and fear, happiness or sadness in others. Ian had no idea why people burst into laughter or into tears.<br><br>- “I wouldn’t expect love from you. I can’t love you back.” <br>Beth plied her fan to her hot face, her heart stumbling. “Hardly flattering, my lord, for a woman to hear a man won’t fall in love with her. She likes to believe she will be the center of his abject devotion.” Mather had said he’d be devoted. The crumpled letter burned her again. <br>“Not won’t. I can’t love you.” <br>“I beg your pardon?” She’d been using the phrase so often tonight. <br>“I am incapable of love. I will not offer it to you.”<br><br>- She studied the sharp profile of his face, the high cheekbones, the square jaw. A woman would want to run her hands through his thick hair when she held him in bed. It would be warm, damp with sweat as he lay heavy-limbed on top of her. <br>Beth dared to reach up and smooth his hair back from his forehead.<br>Ian’s gaze snapped to her. For one instant, he pinned her with his stare. Then his eyes slid sideways. Beth stroked his hair again. <br>He sat still under her touch, quivering with tension like a wild animal. <br><br>- A tear rolled swiftly down her cheek. She put a quick hand on Ian’s, and the piece stumbled to a halt. “You don’t like it,” he said, his voice flat. <br>“I do—only, could you play something a little happier?” <br>Ian’s gaze skimmed past her like a beam of sunlight. “I don’t know whether a piece is happy or sad. I just know the notes.”<br><br>- “When I was first released from the asylum I wouldn’t speak for three months.” He heard her stop behind him. <br>“Oh.” <br>“I hadn’t forgotten how—I simply didn’t want to. I didn’t know it distressed my brothers until they told me. I can’t read hints from others. A person has to tell me a thing plainly.”<br><br>- Ian’s life was dictated by other people—events and conversations swirled past him before he could follow them; other people decided whether he’d live in an asylum or out of it, whether he’d go to Rome or wait in London. Events flowed and ebbed, and as long as they didn’t interfere with his interests, like finding elusive Ming pottery, he let them happen. Now Beth had landed in the swift stream of his life, and she’d stuck there like a rock. Everything else swirled past him, but like an anchor, Beth stayed. He needed her to stay forever.<br><br>- I’m falling in love with you, she wanted to say into their clasped hands. Do you mind awfully?<br><br>- “My memory is too damned good. I can’t blot out things. I want to remember you alone here with me, or in that pension in Paris. You and me, not Fellows or Mather or my brother, or High Holborn . . .” <br>His words died and he began to rub his temple, frustration glinting in his eyes. <br>Beth put her hand over his. “Don’t think of it.” <br>“It plays over and over and over again, like a melody that won’t stop.” <br>Beth softly rubbed his temple, his hard fingers beneath hers. <br>He pulled her close. “Your being with me makes it stop. It’s like the Ming bowls—when I touch them and feel them, everything stops. Nothing matters. You are the same. That is why I brought you here, to keep you with me, where you can please make . . . everything . . . stop.”<br><br>- “Is this what love feels like?” he whispered to her. “I don’t like it, my Beth. It hurts too much.”<i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1442585010ra/16255465.gif" width="350" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></i></i></span>
  <a data-text-id="16857867659673537728" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

    <a title="Starr (AKA Bam Bam) Rivers" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/74622641-starr-aka-bam-bam-rivers"><img alt="Starr (AKA Bam Bam) Rivers" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1581473939p2/74622641.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2566922026?book_show_action=true">Oct 19, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Starr (AKA Bam Bam) Rivers" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Starr (AKA Bam Bam) Rivers" href="/user/show/74622641-starr-aka-bam-bam-rivers">Starr (AKA Bam Bam) Rivers</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/74622641-starr-aka-bam-bam-rivers?shelf=favorite-books">favorite-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/74622641-starr-aka-bam-bam-rivers?shelf=historical-romance">historical-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2566922026" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17510792489736270024">Thanks to Princess Under Cover's recent racy updates: <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='https://www.goodreads.com/user_status/show/198996686?comment=187236616#comment_187236616'>https://www.goodreads.com/user_status...</a><br/><br/>I can't get the Scottie Hottie out of my head! So of course I turned to one of my fav historical Scottish romances, this one.<br/><br/>It's got one of my fav tropes in terms of MCs: a "disabled" unusual Hero - I think he's likely autistic. I love these types of Heroes. 1) I like seeing how their minds work 2) there's a real innocence and purity about them because they don't think the way average people do.<br/><br/>Some ot</span>
  <span id="freeText17510792489736270024" style="display:none">Thanks to Princess Under Cover's recent racy updates: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/user_status/show/198996686?comment=187236616#comment_187236616">https://www.goodreads.com/user_status...</a><br /><br />I can't get the Scottie Hottie out of my head! So of course I turned to one of my fav historical Scottish romances, this one.<br /><br />It's got one of my fav tropes in terms of MCs: a "disabled" unusual Hero - I think he's likely autistic. I love these types of Heroes. 1) I like seeing how their minds work 2) there's a real innocence and purity about them because they don't think the way average people do.<br /><br />Some other readers mentioned that they didn't like Beth, the heroine very much. She was fine for me. I thought she balanced Ian pretty well. She's strong willed, knows what she wants, a little too risk taking, goes with her gut, but then, it takes someone like that to be a good match for Ian. She needs to take care of him.<br /><br />Mostly tho, I love Ian. I love how he has such deep depths of emotion and feeling despite his autism. His rages are because he cares so much. And then when he realizes what love is, the ending tho... made my face about split with a smile!<br /><br />Highly recommend!</span>

<div id="review_1262592277" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1262592277" />
    <a title="Jilly" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/25894509-jilly"><img alt="Jilly" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1435955932p2/25894509.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1262592277?book_show_action=true">Apr 23, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jilly" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jilly" href="/user/show/25894509-jilly">Jilly</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25894509-jilly?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25894509-jilly?shelf=historical-fiction">historical-fiction</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1262592277" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14126955171329320609">When I saw that this historical romance had a lead male character with Asperger's, I just had to read it. I've known a few people with this syndrome and was curious to see how the author would handle the interpersonal relationships between Ian and his loved ones. The people I have known with Asperger's struggle with relationships and have a hard time getting people to understand their mannerisms. Understanding social cues is something that most of us take for granted and don't realize how import</span>
  <span id="freeText14126955171329320609" style="display:none">When I saw that this historical romance had a lead male character with Asperger's, I just had to read it. I've known a few people with this syndrome and was curious to see how the author would handle the interpersonal relationships between Ian and his loved ones. The people I have known with Asperger's struggle with relationships and have a hard time getting people to understand their mannerisms. Understanding social cues is something that most of us take for granted and don't realize how important it is, and how awkward things can be when another person doesn't have this skill. My son's friend with Asperger's is such a sweet kid but has a hard time keeping friends because he doesn't understand things like when it is time to go home, when to wrap up a conversation, and how not to smother another person. It always breaks my heart when he tells us about failed attempts at relationships.<br><br>So, Ian MacKenzie had Asperger's during a time when any deviation from the norm would get a person locked up in an asylum. And, so that is where he spent many years of his life, undergoing horrendous atrocities in the name of "medicine." Luckily, his older brother got him freed from this torture as soon as their father died and he took over the estate. Ian has a brilliant mind and has helped his brother double their family fortune with his perfect memory and mathematical brain.<br><br>Beth is a widow who inherited a fortune from a lady that she had worked for, as a companion. She is engaged to a total player, but doesn't know it. She is trying to get established in London society, and with all of her money, the offers poured in. <br><br><b>
  <i>she liked to laugh that a young widow who'd just come into a good fortune must be, to misquote Jane Austen, in want of a husband.</i>
</b> <br><br>Ian knows her fiance and decides to warn her about what a dog this guy is. Ian is a bit obsessive and finds himself obsessed with her. He proposes to her the very night they meet, but of course she declines. However, she is very intrigued by him... and so it begins.<br><br>Beth is an awesome character because she is amazingly patient and understanding of Ian's eccentricities. She has a way of warming him up and breaking through his barriers - such as the fact that he cannot look into people's eyes or understand jokes.<br><br><b>
  <i>Ian grinned, then burst out laughing...<br>"Beth likes to joke," he said without looking at the others. Beth felt the frost of Hart's rigid stare. Daniel's mouth was open in surprise, and Cameron sat very still. Something had happened, and Beth wasn't certain what...<br>..."Tell me something, Daniel," Beth said. "In the dining room, when Ian laughed at me, you all stared like the ceiling had come down. Why?"<br>Daniel wrinkled his forehead. "Why? 'Twas because Ian laughed. I don't think any of us have ever heard Uncle Ian laugh out loud before."</i>
</b><br><br><a href="http://photobucket.com/images/the%20feels" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1419374448ra/13047936.gif" alt="the feels photo: Loki Feels lokifeels.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>That was so sweet. She keeps breaking through to him and it is heartwarming. But, I do like that the author doesn't "heal" him and have him suddenly stop having Asperger's. That would have ruined the story because it isn't realistic. Beth just helps Ian function at a higher level with her unconditional love and patience - she doesn't (and cannot) "fix" him. <br><br>Not all of Ian's problems are Asperger's related, though. He is suspected of murder, and has been very traumatized by his past. There is a mystery wrapped up in the story, and Ian is terrified that Beth is in danger. However, Beth is a smart and resourceful person. She wants to clear Ian's name and is determined to help him.<br><br>The only negative thing in the book, to me, was that there was some weird sexual language. Maybe it is Scottish lingo, but it threw me. Other than that, I loved the overall story and characters of Ian and Beth.</span>
  <a data-text-id="14126955171329320609" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_3409157942" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3409157942" />
    <a title="Jessica " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4844580-jessica"><img alt="Jessica " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1494278516p2/4844580.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3409157942?book_show_action=true">Jun 27, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jessica " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jessica " href="/user/show/4844580-jessica">Jessica </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4844580-jessica?shelf=historical-romance">historical-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4844580-jessica?shelf=needs-review">needs-review</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4844580-jessica?shelf=damaged-hero">damaged-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4844580-jessica?shelf=audiobook">audiobook</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3409157942" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12886188549646892714">SO MANY people have told me that I need to read this book because of how much I love Scottish historical romances. I finally got the audiobook from my library and COULD NOT STOP until I was finished with this book. <br/><br/>Immediately when this book started, I fell in love with Ian's character. It's not explicitly stated, but it is inferred that Ian is on the autism spectrum and no one in society knows what to do with him. He spent a lot of his life in asylums and being degraded by his father because of</span>
  <span id="freeText12886188549646892714" style="display:none">SO MANY people have told me that I need to read this book because of how much I love Scottish historical romances. I finally got the audiobook from my library and COULD NOT STOP until I was finished with this book. <br /><br />Immediately when this book started, I fell in love with Ian's character. It's not explicitly stated, but it is inferred that Ian is on the autism spectrum and no one in society knows what to do with him. He spent a lot of his life in asylums and being degraded by his father because of the way he was. I loved how close he was to his bothers and how protective they were over Ian, especially because they had no control over what had happened to him when he was younger. I loved how Beth actually loved those aspects of Ian's personality that people were scared of and how she was never scared off from him like so many people are. <br /><br />I really loved the pacing of the relationship between Ian and Beth. It just started off of as attraction and heat and slowly developed into something more. They obviously cared for each other, but Ian thought he wasn't capable of ever loving someone. My heart broke for Ian throughout this whole book and I just wanted him to be happy. And I loved how Beth was a widow. I haven't run across many romances with a widow, so I enjoyed that aspect and how she had more freedom as a woman to explore a relationship with Ian because she had already been married. <br /><br />If you can't tell, I absolutely loved this book. I am so excited to read the rest of the Mackenzie's stories because I fell in love with all of their characters in this book. I highly recommend you pick this up! </span>
  <a data-text-id="12886188549646892714" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_480770620" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/480770620" />
    <a title="Richa" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2796667-richa"><img alt="Richa" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1354430575p2/2796667.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/480770620?book_show_action=true">Dec 18, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Richa" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Richa" href="/user/show/2796667-richa">Richa</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Richa by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/8310179-blacky-romance-addict">Blacky *Romance Addict*</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer480770620" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17116250259869056149"><i><b>“Here's to the crazy ones. The misfits. The rebels. The troublemakers. The round pegs in the square holes. The ones who see things differently.</b> They're not fond of rules. And they have no respect for the status quo. You can quote them, disagree with them, glorify or vilify them. About the only thing you can't do is ignore them...."</i> <br/><br/><b>Year: 1881<br/><br/><u>MADNESS</u><br/><br/>Some people are mad in love....<br/><br/><i>When love is not madness, it is not love.</i><br/><span>[image error]</span><br/><br/>Some are mad in passion....<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401332i/778839._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Some are mad in obsession....<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401332i/778840.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>And some</b></span>
  <span id="freeText17116250259869056149" style="display:none"><i><b>“Here's to the crazy ones. The misfits. The rebels. The troublemakers. The round pegs in the square holes. The ones who see things differently.</b> They're not fond of rules. And they have no respect for the status quo. You can quote them, disagree with them, glorify or vilify them. About the only thing you can't do is ignore them...."</i> <br><br><b>Year: 1881<br><br><u>MADNESS</u><br><br>Some people are mad in love....<br><br><i>When love is not madness, it is not love.</i><br><span>[image error]</span><br><br>Some are mad in passion....<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401332i/778839._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Some are mad in obsession....<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401332i/778840.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And some are simply mad....<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401332i/778841.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>He is all of the above and more....<br><br><span>[image error]</span><br><br>He is different from the other people....unique, or as people would say mad....<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401332i/778843._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The smallest of things fascinate him.....hold him captive...intrigue him...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401332i/778844.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Ming bowls and beautiful women are his areas of interest....<i>huge</i> areas of interest....<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401332i/778845._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>He remembers <i>everything</i>.....he might not be able to understand certain things but he never forgets......he's a highly complex yet a very simple man...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401332i/778846.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>He has a tortured past</b>, a <i>horribly</i> painful past,.....an insane past....and secrets...which torture him all the time...a past which makes him feel incapable of ever loving somebody...anybody...<br><br><b><i>“I am incapable of love. I will not offer it to you.” <br><br>Beth wondered what was more heartbreaking, the words themselves or the flat tone of voice with which he delivered them.</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401332i/778847.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>He's the kind of man who usually lets his life flow around him but when he wants something...he makes sure he gets it....nothing can stop him from having it....<br><br><span>[image error]</span><br><br>He is Ian Mackenzie....the youngest brother in the notorious Mackenzie family....a family known for it's past...a past filled intrigue, drama and scandal enough to last centuries....<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401332i/778849.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And this time he wants <i>her</i>....Beth Ackerley...from the very first moment he lays his eyes on her.....<i>because she is the most beautiful thing he'd ever seen in his life</i>...and he's going to have her by hook or by crook...</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401332i/778850._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Beth Ackerley is a widow...a widow who has recently come into a fortune...she is a woman as intrigued by the youngest Mackenzie as he is by her....as attracted to him as he is to her...<br><br><b>
  <i>I do not think of him as Lord Ian Mackenzie, aristocratic brother of a duke and well beyond my reach; not as the Mad Mackenzie, an eccentric people stare at and whisper about.<br><br>To me, he is simply Ian.</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401332i/778851._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><span>[image error]</span><br><br>But will she succumb to this inexplicable, instant, undeniable attraction that she feels for him??<br><br><b><i>She wanted this—no maidenly vapors, no shrinking away from him. Beth Ackerley knew what it was to be with a man, and she liked it. His body throbbed with possibilities. <br><br>“We should stop,” she whispered.<br><br>“Do you want to stop?”<br><br>“Now that you mention it, not really.”<br><br>“Then why?” His lips brushed her mouth as he spoke. She tasted whiskey on his tongue, felt the firm brush of his lips, the roughness of his chin. He had a man’s mouth, a commanding mouth.<br><br>“I’m sure there are a dozen reasons why we should stop. I confess I can’t think of any good ones at the moment.”</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401332i/778853._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>What will she do when she realises that he wants to possess her....in <i>every possible way</i>....mind, body, and soul....???<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401332i/778854.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>What will she do when she realises that someone is after him, ready to destroy him...??<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401332i/778855.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Well that's for me to know and you to find out!! ;)<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401332i/778856.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>Ian touched a lock of hair that had drifted to her forehead.<br><br>“You are real.”<br><br>The touch had her heart pounding and heat washing to every limb. He sat too close, his fingertips so warm through his gloves. It would be a simple thing to tilt her head back and kiss him.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401332i/778857.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>“I am a wicked, wicked woman,” she murmured. “Kiss me again.” Without a word he swiftly slanted his lips over hers. His tongue stabbed inside her mouth, and he pressed his fingers to the corners of her lips, opening her wider. These weren’t the kisses of a man flirting. They were the kisses of a man who wanted to lie with her, damn the timing and damn the circumstances. Every part of her that touched him throbbed.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401332i/778858.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>He would soon arrange it so he never had to leave. He’d marry her for a very basic reason: to have her with him every night, every day, every afternoon, and every time in between.<br><br>He walked down the boulevard, something in him awakening and breaking free.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401332i/778859.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>“What was it like?” His words were so low she barely caught them. “Explain to me what loving feels like, Beth. I want to understand.”<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401332i/778860.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Ian’s life was dictated by other people—events and conversations swirled past him before he could follow them; other people decided whether he’d live in an asylum or out of it, whether he’d go to Rome or wait in London. Events flowed and ebbed, and as long as they didn’t interfere with his interests, like finding elusive Ming pottery, he let them happen.<br><br>Now Beth had landed in the swift stream of his life, and she’d stuck there like a rock.<br><br>Everything else swirled past him, but like an anchor, Beth stayed.<br><br>He needed her to stay forever.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401332i/778861.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>"....When you love, especially with all your heart, it comes upon you so fast, you don’t have time to resist.”<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401332i/778862.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>He pulled her close. “Your being with me makes it stop. It’s like the Ming bowls—when I touch them and feel them, everything stops. Nothing matters. You are the same. That is why I brought you here, to keep you with me, where you can please make...everything . . . stop.”<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401332i/778863.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Beth touched his face. “Ian.”<br><br>He loved how she said his name. She spoke the syllables gently, her voice always soft, caressing.<br><br>Hart loomed up behind her, but Ian dissolved into Beth. He slid his arms around her waist and buried his face in her neck.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401332i/778864.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>“Is this what love feels like?” he whispered to her. “I don’t like it, my Beth. It hurts too much.”<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401332i/778865.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Beth’s thoughts went to when she’d wakened in the night, when Ian had looked straight down into her eyes. His golden gaze had been so anguished, so filled with pain. Now his gaze was evasive again, not letting her catch it. “It’s not fair that you look at me only when I’m extremely ill,” Beth said. “Now that I am fully awake and feeling better, you turn away.”<br><br>“Because when I look at you, I forget everything. I lose all track of what I’m saying or doing. I can see only your eyes.” He laid his head on her pillow and rested his hand on her chest. “You have such beautiful eyes.” <br><br>Her heart beat faster. “And then you flatter me so that I’ll feel awful that I chided you.”<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401332i/778866.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>"My Beth,” he whispered, his breath hot on her swollen lips. “Thank you.”<br><br>“For what?” Beth couldn’t stop crying, but she smiled, her face aching with it.<br><br>“Setting me free.”</i></b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401332i/778867.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>It was a very enjoyable historical romance. <b>I loved the hero!! Ian was adorable, lovable and made me fall for him with every line that he said...every line that he thought...and he was ok, I'm fumbling around for words here because he is just that good!! That amazing....sweet, lovely, wonderful, awesome...well, you get my point, right? ;)<br><br>Beth was a truly remarkable heroine...she was strong, independent and completely in love with Ian which made me love her all the more! :)<br><br>I truly enjoyed reading about the other characters and the glimpse that we get of each brother's tragic story....it is a family of 4 handsome, crazy in their own way brothers whose lives filled with dramas and suspense...each brother battling his own demons.</b><br><br>My only complaint with it is that it (the story) felt a little bit rushed...I mean things happened too quickly to be believable sometimes and the flow of the story wasn't very smooth because of it. But all of my complaints vanished when I read the parts in which Ian's perspective was shown...I loved this story!! <b>Especially Ian (of course)!! He made me want to reach inside the book and hug him so hard and protect him from anything and everything that might hurt him...but hey, Beth was already there...so, I guess that makes my role kind of redundant. :P I choked up when I read about the kind of things he had to suffer in the asylum....it was aghhhhhhhhhhhh......</b><br><br>I don't know if this might be spoiler or not, but putting it under a spoiler alert anyway to be on the safe side. The madness that is referred to in the title is about his <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ autism. He suffers from the Asperger syndrome (AS). Also known as Asperger's syndrome or Asperger disorder, it is an autism spectrum disorder (ASD) that is characterized by significant difficulties in social interaction, alongside restricted and repetitive patterns of behavior and interests. It differs from other autism spectrum disorders by its relative preservation of linguistic and cognitive development. (according to wikipedia). <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> There are a few inconsistencies in the story regarding this and the mystery which pops up in the story is not that big of a mystery either but despite all this it's <b>a very romantic and sweet story which I would recommend to EVERYONE!!! :)</b><br><br>This was my first Jennifer Ashley book and it's definitely not going to be the last. :) Hope I get time to read more because real life's really taking up a LOT of my time... :((<br><br>But anyway....<br><br><b>I LOVED IT!!!!! Ian *sigh*.....<br><br>In a completely sane world, madness is the only freedom! And love the only way..... :)<br><br>And we're all a little crazy, aren't we?.....</b>(Ok, in my case maybe a bit more than little...but whatever...that's just semantics... :P)<br> <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401332i/778868._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>So, you go and enjoy this lovely, wonderful story while I dream of <i>him</i>....<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401332ra/778869.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Enjoy!! :)</b></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_113404297" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/113404297" />
    <a title="Laura" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2043222-laura"><img alt="Laura" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1577660807p2/2043222.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/113404297?book_show_action=true">Jul 25, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Laura" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Laura" href="/user/show/2043222-laura">Laura</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2043222-laura?shelf=highlander-books">highlander-books</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer113404297" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15333777854180399177">I was super excited to read this book, seeing as everyone loved this book, and I love Jennifer Ashley/Allyson James. I was not disappointed. This has one of the best storylines I've ever read. I won't summarize since so many people have reviewed and/or summarized, but can I just say "Wow."<br/><br/>Lord Ian Mackenzie is the youngest of 4 brothers and he has a slight disability. He doesn't understand emotion. For example, he can play a piano piece perfectly after only having heard it once, but he can't fee</span>
  <span id="freeText15333777854180399177" style="display:none">I was super excited to read this book, seeing as everyone loved this book, and I love Jennifer Ashley/Allyson James. I was not disappointed. This has one of the best storylines I've ever read. I won't summarize since so many people have reviewed and/or summarized, but can I just say "Wow."<br /><br />Lord Ian Mackenzie is the youngest of 4 brothers and he has a slight disability. He doesn't understand emotion. For example, he can play a piano piece perfectly after only having heard it once, but he can't feel the emotion behind it. Or he knows that one applauds after a show, or at the opera, but he doesn't get why. Lord Ian is intelligent, highly so..a genius with numbers and odds, so an acquaintance of his asks his opinion on his bride-to-be. Lord Ian has her investigated, and he feels Beth is too good for the likes of Mather. so not only does he tell her, he proposes. it was a great scene. Fantastic, and this whole book was above and beyond my expectations. <br /><br />Beth, however, decides Ian can't possibly be serious, and goes off to Paris. Well Lord Ian follows. But not before having a few scandalous episodes that Beth spots in the London Post society section. Lord Ian harbors a couple big secrets, really big ones, and not only is the Inspector way off in his deluded case of "justice," but so is everyone else's opinions. One secret (and not a "spoiler" secret)is that his father killed his mother in front of him in a fit of rage, and at 12, he had Ian committed. Ian was never mad, but he was different. And he was so worked up that at the sanity hearing (mind you he was 12 and had just watched his father shake his mother to death!) he could only rock and repeat the same phrase from a poem over and over to calm himself. So of course, he is committed. Luckily his brother gets him out after their father dies, but Ian had been locked up for something like 10 years or so (I forget the actual number). The electro shock therapy, the cold ice baths, the beatings, all of it, had taken it's toll, and yet Ian remained a remarkable man. He has rages, like when he sees the vengeance-driven Inspector Fellows talking to Beth, but he really is afraid he'll rage against Beth. <br /><br />The romance between the two is fabulous, as is the passion. I like how Beth's husband (her first husband) was a good man, and she was able to still love him, but be passionately in love with Ian as well. I loved the Mackenzie clan. even Isabella, Mac's estranged wife. We see her when Beth goes to Paris. And just as we think Ian is in front of Beth, it turns out to be one of his brothers, Mac Mackenzie. Mac is keeping tabs on his wife. Their story is next, and also fabulous!!<br />The only thing I didn't like about this book was Inspector Fellows. The surprise twist at the end was good, and well played, but I couldn't muster enough emotion for Fellows after the way he had harangued Ian and Beth. <br /><br />(I meant this review to be short...ha!)<br /><br />I loved how Beth was able to hold her own with Hart...he was such a jerk to her, and yet she was able to make Ian laugh...that was a miracle in and of itself since he usually didn't understand humor. At the end, Ian still couldn't understand a lot of jokes, or follow a conversation with more than one or two people, but he'd gotten better at making eye contact, and he fell in love with Beth...there is a side story of a murder from 5 years before (hence Inspector Fellows' obsession with bringing Ian down) and then a similar murder right after Ian and Beth met. But anyways, I tell you this so you understand when I say that Beth is injured in her quest to clear Ian, and Ian finally understands that without Beth he has nothing, and feels nothing. It was simply amazing to watch his transformation and his and Beth's romance. When he tells her he loves her, and it becomes "Iloveyou.loveyou.loveyou.loveyou." It was beautiful.<br /><br />I. LOVED. THIS. BOOK.<br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.demonloversbooksandmore.com/2011/07/winner.html">http://www.demonloversbooksandmore.co...</a><br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="15333777854180399177" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4878104-kat?shelf=i-sinned-i-skimmed">i-sinned-i-skimmed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4878104-kat?shelf=dude-where-is-the-plot">dude-where-is-the-plot</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4878104-kat?shelf=m-f">m-f</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer405158801" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12666246679742300334">I had no idea what a <i>cunny</i> was and why the hero wanted to kiss it, but now I do.<br/><br/>Meet Ian. The mad MacKenzie.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380389776ra/751089.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>He apparently suffers from Aspergers syndrome. I can't say that I wasn't interested to discover how that would work out; a fluffy romance hero with a mental condition to swoon over. But my starting point was expecting to enjoy the interesting edge that Ian's autism would bring to the story. <br/><br/>There's so much going on in <i>The Madness of Lord Ian Mackenzie</i> though, none of which is executed prop</span>
  <span id="freeText12666246679742300334" style="display:none">I had no idea what a <i>cunny</i> was and why the hero wanted to kiss it, but now I do.<br><br>Meet Ian. The mad MacKenzie.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380389776ra/751089.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>He apparently suffers from Aspergers syndrome. I can't say that I wasn't interested to discover how that would work out; a fluffy romance hero with a mental condition to swoon over. But my starting point was expecting to enjoy the interesting edge that Ian's autism would bring to the story. <br><br>There's so much going on in <i>The Madness of Lord Ian Mackenzie</i> though, none of which is executed properly. Ian's mental issues are completely downplayed. He is just your typical barbarian, who follows his <i>swollen organ</i> and is hardly able to utter a coherent sentence. Why he and the meh heroine, Beth, are instantly infatuated with each other remains a riddle. Their sudden love is never explained by the author, other than that Ian finds Beth <i>beautiful</i> and she appreciates his rock-hard bod and <i> amber eyes like brandy, flecked with gold as though the sun danced on them.</i> <br><br>Shortly after having met Ian, the heroine takes off to Paris to learn how to paint. Upon her arrival she accidentally bumps into, somewhere on top of a random hill, Ian's brother. Who happens to be a painter no less! Beth then also meets his gorgeous ex-wife Annabella, who takes her under her wings immediately and - again without the author making any of it appear plausible - the two become besties. Then - surprise! - Ian pops up in Paris...<br><br>I'm a sucker for the courtship rituals that this genre often offers; the Old World politeness, the amusing banter as the slightly sarcastic hero and the heroine are trying to outwit each other, the games of pushing and pulling... Since in this book I was stuck with a hero who could not even process humor, emotions and conversations, I was obviously out of luck. <br><br>Still, I would like to finish on a amusing note. So it's time to move on to the <i>sweet berries, swollen organs</i> and <i>wanton hands</i>! What about this rather unconventional erotic scene?<br><br><i>"Are you wet?" Ian whispered, teeth on her earlobe. <br>"Yes." She tried to swallow. "If you must know, I am quite, quite damp."<br>"Good." His hot tongue circled the shell of her ear. "You understand such things. Why you need to be wet."<br>"My husband explained on our wedding night. He thought that ignorance on the woman's part was the cause of much unnecessary pain."<br>(...) He wanted Beth to apply her mouth to his nipples, then let her sink down to her knees to take his staff into her clever mouth and practice giving him love bites there. At last his clothes parted, and she was able to reveal that part of a man's anatomy that is the cause of so much wickedness." </i></span>
  <a data-text-id="12666246679742300334" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_445666304" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/445666304" />
    <a title="Penny" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7463065-penny"><img alt="Penny" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1420145167p2/7463065.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/445666304?book_show_action=true">Oct 31, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Penny" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Penny" href="/user/show/7463065-penny">Penny</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="MP3 CD 9781452656922" href="/book/show/13558312-the-madness-of-lord-ian-mackenzie">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7463065-penny?shelf=reviewed">reviewed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7463065-penny?shelf=h-read-historical-romance">h-read-historical-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer445666304" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8393814061483784564">It's ok. <br/><br/>This story is fine, but is not a book I'll be remembering after a while. <br/><br/>I have only given a few historical romance books more than three stars. Maybe it's not the best romance genre for me, or maybe I should't "read" them through audiobooks, I don't know, but I usually don't find them remarkable enough. <br/>However, I keep reading them because three of my favorite romance books of all time are historical romances and I keep hoping I'll find some other book in this genre that will move me a</span>
  <span id="freeText8393814061483784564" style="display:none">It's ok. <br /><br />This story is fine, but is not a book I'll be remembering after a while. <br /><br />I have only given a few historical romance books more than three stars. Maybe it's not the best romance genre for me, or maybe I should't "read" them through audiobooks, I don't know, but I usually don't find them remarkable enough. <br />However, I keep reading them because three of my favorite romance books of all time are historical romances and I keep hoping I'll find some other book in this genre that will move me as those three did: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/14386.If_You_Dare__MacCarrick_Brothers___1_" title="If You Dare (MacCarrick Brothers, #1) by Kresley Cole" rel="nofollow noopener">If You Dare</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/420782.If_You_Desire__MacCarrick_Brothers___2_" title="If You Desire (MacCarrick Brothers, #2) by Kresley Cole" rel="nofollow noopener">If You Desire</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/420780.If_You_Deceive__MacCarrick_Brothers___3_" title="If You Deceive (MacCarrick Brothers, #3) by Kresley Cole" rel="nofollow noopener">If You Deceive</a> from the MacCarrick Brother Trilogy by <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/4428.Kresley_Cole" title="Kresley Cole" rel="nofollow noopener">Kresley Cole</a>. <br /><br />I don't have much to say about this book, I know many people loved it, but I didn't find the characters that likable or the romance in it unforgettable. <br /><br />In fact, <b>the romance wasn't very nice</b>. I didn't like the way he was instantly ready to marry her after a minute of "meeting" each other. I didn't like the circumstances in which they married. I don't get why or how she fell in love with him. There is not a moment where they have a communicative, honest and trustworthy relationship between each other.<br /><br />Ian was too peculiar and vulnerable to be appealing to me. He was interesting from a character perspective, but not from a sexual way; and when I read a romance, both requirements are necessary for me in the male MC. I find attractive a radically different kind of man than Lord Ian is. I like them more confident and resourceful, domineering in an alpha male kind of way but not like Ian, not by being a pushy dictator; and very importantly, of sound mind, definitely not to one with some kind of mild autism like Ian Mackenzie seems to have. Add to that that he is traumatized and severely damaged and you have a completely unappealing package for me.<br /><br />Beth behaves during the whole book like a very trustful person, manageable and not very bright, except at the end of course, when she suddenly solves three miseries in a row by her lone self.<br /><br />I don't think I'll continue this series, but if I do I'll try not to listen to the audiobooks because they definitely work in its detriment; I just don't know if I have the patience for it (for actually reading the books I mean).</span>
  <a data-text-id="8393814061483784564" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer396579503" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer696313054863411461"><b>Ian is a good man...</b><br/><br/>I can't write a review for this story, I just can't. There is no way I can do it justice. I read this one years ago and it touched me in a way that many books miss by a smidge. Your heart beats for a man who has spent years frustrated by his perceived shortcomings, yet not able to change. These characters come alive for me and I find myself looking at the siblings like a parent. I wanted to knock their heads together one minute, then call for a group hug the next.<br/><br/>The love sto</span>
  <span id="freeText696313054863411461" style="display:none"><b>Ian is a good man...</b><br /><br />I can't write a review for this story, I just can't. There is no way I can do it justice. I read this one years ago and it touched me in a way that many books miss by a smidge. Your heart beats for a man who has spent years frustrated by his perceived shortcomings, yet not able to change. These characters come alive for me and I find myself looking at the siblings like a parent. I wanted to knock their heads together one minute, then call for a group hug the next.<br /><br />The love story is an original and there aren't too many authors who can capture the emotions as well. There's a connection and understanding between Ian and Beth that others would be jealous of. Such dedication and love mixed with possessiveness and desperation to be near each other. It's appealing yet also could be stifling. Only certain people could cope.<br /><br />The narrator does a fabulous job and I never struggled to tell the characters apart. No change in the ratings, I loved both the read and the audio.<br /><br />Love this one and I can't help but go on and see Mac try to get the love of his life back.</span>
  <a data-text-id="696313054863411461" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
